<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смять.html>смять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сминать.html>смина́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rumple, to crumple, to wrinkle, to fumble, to crease</li></ol>

***снаружи.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снаружи.html>снару́жи</a> (4633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снаружи.html>снару́жи</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snarúži</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>on the outside, from the outside, outwardly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отворяться.html>отворя́ется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снаружи.html>снару́жи</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oknó otvorjájetsja <b>snarúži</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">The window opens from the outside.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кнару́жи</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">knarúži</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снаряд.html>снаря́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snarjád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снаряд.html>снаря́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снаряд.html>снаря́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снаряд.html>снаря́дов</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нарядить.html>наряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">narjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снаряжать.html>снаряжа́ть</a> (28765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снарядить.html>снаряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">snarjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снаряжать.html>снаряжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snarjažátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снарядить.html>снаряди́ть</a></b>)

<li><i>(an expedition, a search party etc.)</i> to send, to dispatch</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>снасть</a> (14785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>снасть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снасть.html>сна́сти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снасть.html>сна́сти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снасть.html>сна́стей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tackle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыболовный.html>рыболо́вная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>снасть</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rybolóvnaja <b>snastʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fishing tackle</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <span class="deprecated-label">usually in the plural</span></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rope, rigging</li></ol>

***снег.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a> (457)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sněgъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*snóygʷʰos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sneg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>сне́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снега́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снего́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>snow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идёт</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idjót <b>sneg</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is snowing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мокрый.html>мо́крый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mókryj <b>sneg</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">sleet, wet snow</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скидывать.html>ски́дывать</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:скинуть.html>ски́нуть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skídyvatʹ/skínutʹ <b>sneg</b> s krýši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw <b>the snow</b> off the roof</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́лову</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>sneg</b> na gólovu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">like a bolt from the blue <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">unexpectedly, suddenly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">like snow on the head</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">что́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлогодний.html>прошлого́дний</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">štó-libo núžno, kak prošlogódnij <b>sneg</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">something is not needed in the least</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">something is needed like last year's snow</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зимо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>сне́га</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выпросить.html>вы́просить</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">saying</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zimój <b>snéga</b> ne výprositʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><span class="use-with-mention">(said about somebody mean, stingy)</span></span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">cannot be asked for snow in winter</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поваляться.html>поваля́емся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снегу́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Daváj povaljájemsja v <b>snegú</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Let's roll in the snow!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> snow, the white electrical noise on a TV set when there is no TV signal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cocaine</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снеговик.html>снегови́к</a> (28111)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снеговик.html>снегови́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snegovík</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снеговик.html>снеговика́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снеговик.html>снеговики́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снеговик.html>снеговико́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>snowman (figure made of snow)</li></ol>

***снегопад.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снегопад.html>снегопад</a> (12429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1899. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снег.html>снег</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sneg</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">snow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́д(ать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pád(atʹ)</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; possibly a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schneefall</i>.
</p>

***снести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снести.html>снести́</a> (5212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снести.html>снести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сносить.html>сноси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry down</li>
<li>to carry to</li>
<li>to pull down, to demolish</li>
<li>to blow off, to blow away <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the wind</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to carry away <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to tolerate, to endure</li>
<li>to cut off</li>
<li>to discard (a card)</li>
<li>to lay eggs
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нести.html>нести́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снижать.html>снижа́ющий</a> (9053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:снижение.html>сниже́ние</a> (3781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снизить.html>сни́зить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">snízitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снижение.html>сниже́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">snižénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снижение.html>сниже́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снижение.html>сниже́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снижение.html>сниже́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>reduction, decrease <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">act, process, or result of reducing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<li>lowering</li>
<li>descent (<i>aviation</i>)</li></ol>
